firstException.compareAndSet(null, invokeOnAssignment(assignor, assignment));\n456: \n457:         // Reschedule the auto commit starting from now\n458:         if (autoCommitEnabled)\n459: previously owned but are now assigned\n464:         firstException.compareAndSet(null, rebalanceListenerInvoker.invokePartitionsAssigned(addedPartitions));\n465: \n466:         if (firstException.get() != null) {\n467:             if (firstException.get() instanceof KafkaException) {\n468:                 throw (KafkaException) firstException.get();\n469:             } else {\n470:                 throw new KafkaException(\"User rebalance callback throws an error\", firstException.get());\n471:             }\n472:         }\n473:     }\n474: \n475:     void !ensureCoordinatorReadyAsync();\n495:     }\n496: \n497:     /**\n498:      * Poll for coordinator events. This ensures that the coordinator is known and that the consumer\n499:      * has joined the group (if it is using group management). This also handles periodic offset commits\n500:      * if they are enabled.\n501:      * <p>\n502:      * Returns early if the timeout expires or if waiting on rejoin is not required\n503:      *\n504:      * @param timer Timer bounding how long this method can block\n505:      * @param waitForJoinGroup Boolean flag indicating if we should wait until re-join group completes\n506:      * @throws KafkaException if the rebalance callback throws an exception\n507:      * @return true iff the operation succeeded\n508:      */\n509:     public boolean poll(Timer timer, boolean waitForJoinGroup) {\n510:         maybeUpdateSubscriptionMetadata();\n511: \n512:         invokeCompletedOffsetCommitCallbacks();\n513: \n514:         if (subscriptions.hasAutoAssignedPartitions()) {\n515:             if (protocol == null) {\n516:                 throw new IllegalStateException(\"User configured \" + ConsumerConfig.PARTITION_ASSIGNMENT_STRATEGY_CONFIG +\n517:                     \" to empty while trying to subscribe for group protocol to auto assign partitions\");\n518:             }\n519:             // Always update the heartbeat last poll time so that the heartbeat thread does not leave the\n520:             // group proactively due to application inactivity even if (say) the coordinator cannot be found.\n521:             pollHeartbeat(timer.currentTimeMs());\n522:             if (coordinatorUnknownAndUnreadySync(timer)) {\n523:                 return false;\n524:             }\n525: \n526:             if (rejoinNeededOrPending()) {\n527:                 // due to a race condition between the initial metadata fetch and the initial rebalance,\n528:                 // we need to ensure that the metadata is fresh before joining initially. This ensures\n529:                 // that we have matched the pattern against the cluster's topics at least once before joining.\n530:                 if (subscriptions.hasPatternSubscription()) {\n531:                     // For consumer group that uses pattern-based subscription, after a topic is created,\n532:                     // any consumer that discovers the topic after metadata refresh can trigger rebalance\n533:                     // across the entire consumer group. Multiple rebalances can be triggered after one topic\n534:                     // creation if consumers refresh metadata at vastly different times. We can significantly\n535:                     // reduce the number of rebalances caused by single topic creation by asking consumer to\n536:                     // refresh metadata before re-joining the group as long as the refresh backoff time has\n537:                     // passed.\n538:                     if (this.metadata.timeToAllowUpdate(timer.currentTimeMs()) == 0) {\n539:                         this.metadata.requestUpdate(true);\n540:                     }\n541: \n542:                     if (!client.ensureFreshMetadata(timer)) {\n543:                         return false;\n544:                     }\n545: \n546:                     maybeUpdateSubscriptionMetadata();\n547:                 }\n548: \n549:                 // if not wait for join group, we would just use a timer of 0\n550:                 if (!ensureActiveGroup(waitForJoinGroup ? timer : time.timer(0L))) {\n551:                     // since we may use a different timer in the callee, we'd still need\n552:                     // to update the original timer's current time after the call\n553:                     timer.update(time.milliseconds());\n554: \n555:                     return false;\n556:                 }\n557:             }\n558:         } else {\n559:             // For manually assigned partitions, we do not try to pro-actively lookup coordinator;\n560:             // instead we only try to refresh metadata when necessary.\n561:             // If connections to all nodes fail, wakeups triggered while attempting to send fetch\n562:             // requests result in polls returning immediately, causing a tight loop of polls. Without\n563:             // the wakeup, poll() with no channels would block for the timeout, delaying re-connection.\n564:             // awaitMetadataUpdate() in ensureCoordinatorReady initiates new connections with configured backoff and avoids the busy loop.\n565:             if (metadata.updateRequested() && !client.hasReadyNodes(timer.currentTimeMs())) {\n566:                 client.awaitMetadataUpdate(timer);\n567:             }\n568: \n569:             // if there is pending coordinator requests, ensure they have a chance to be transmitted.\n570:             client.pollNoWakeup();\n571:         }\n572: \n573:         maybeAutoCommitOffsetsAsync(timer.currentTimeMs());\n574:         return true;\n575:     }\n576: \n577:     /**\n578:      * Return the time wait before the next invocation of poll()\n581:      */\n582:     public long timeToNextPoll(long now) {\n583:         if (!autoCommitEnabled)\n584:             return timeToNextHeartbeat(now);\n585: \n586:         return Math.min(nextAutoCommitTimer.remainingMs(), timeToNextHeartbeat(now));\n587:     }\n588: \n589:     private void updateGroupSubscription(Set<String> topics) {\n590:         // assignments returned by the assignor such that no owned partitions are going to\n718:      * be reassigned to a different consumer directly: if the assignor wants to reassign an owned partition,\n719:      * it must first remove it from the new assignment of the current owner so that it is not assigned to any\n720:      * member, and then in the next rebalance it can finally reassign those partitions not owned by anyone to consumers.\n721:      */\n722:     private void validateCooperativeAssignment(final Map<String, List<TopicPartition>> ownedPartitions,\n723:                                                final Map<String, Assignment> assignments) {\n724:         Set<TopicPartition> totalRevokedPartitions = new HashSet<>();\n725:         SortedSet<TopicPartition> totalAddedPartitions = new TreeSet<>(COMPARATOR);\n726:         for (final Map.Entry<String, Assignment> entry : assignments.entrySet()) {\n727:             final Assignment assignment = entry.getValue();\n728:             final Set<TopicPartition> addedPartitions = new HashSet<>(assignment.partitions());\n729:             addedPartitions.removeAll(ownedPartitions.get(entry.getKey()));\n730:             final Set<TopicPartition> revokedPartitions = new HashSet<>(ownedPartitions.get(entry.getKey()));\n731: private void maybeMarkPartitionsPendingRevocation() {\n865:         if (protocol != RebalanceProtocol.EAGER) {\n866:             return;\n867:         }\n868: \n869:         // When asynchronously {}\", partitions);\n877:         subscriptions.markPendingRevocation(partitions);\n878:     }\n879: \n880:     @Override\n881:     public void onLeavePrepare() {\n882:         // Save the current @Override\n913:     public boolean rejoinNeededOrPending() {\n914:         if (!subscriptions.hasAutoAssignedPartitions())\n915:             return false;\n916: \n917:         // we need to rejoin if \n937:     /**\n938:      * Refresh the committed offsets for partitions that require initialization.\n939:      *\n940:      * @param timer Timer bounding how long this method can block\n941:      * operation timed out\n960:      */\n961:     public Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> fetchCommittedOffsets(final Set<TopicPartition> partitions,\n962:                                                                         final Timer timer) {\n963:         if (partitions.isEmpty()) return Collections.emptyMap();\n964: \n965:         final Generation generationForOffsetRequest = generationIfStable();\n966:         if (pendingCommittedOffsetRequest != null &&\n967:             !pendingCommittedOffsetRequest.sameRequest(partitions, generationForOffsetRequest)) {\n968:    }\n996:             } else {\n997:                 return null;\n998:             }\n999:         } while (timer.notExpired());\n1000:         return null;\n1001:     }\n1002: \n1003:     /**\n1004:      * Return the consumer group metadata.\n1005:      *\n1006:      * @return the current consumer group metadata\n1007:      */\n1008:     public ConsumerGroupMetadata groupMetadata() {\n1009:         return groupMetadata;\n1010:     }\n1011: \n1012:     /**\n1013:      * @throws KafkaException if the rebalance callback throws exception\n1014:      */\n1015:     public void    ensureCoordinatorReady(timer);\n1022:                 client.poll(timer);\n1023:                 invokeCompletedOffsetCommitCallbacks();\n1024:             }\n1025:         } finally {\n1026:             super.close(timer, membershipOperation);\n1027:         }\n1028:     }\n1029: \n1030:     // visible for testing\n1031:     void invokeCompletedOffsetCommitCallbacks() {\n1032:         if (asyncCommitFenced.get()) {\n1033:             throw new FencedInstanceIdException(\"Get fenced exception for group.instance.id \"\n1034:                 + rebalanceConfig.groupInstanceId.orElse(\"unset_instance_id\")\n1035:                 + \", current member.id is \" + memberId());\n1036:         }\n1037:         while (true) {\n1038: completion.invoke();\n1043:         }\n1044:     }\n1045: \n1046:     public RequestFuture<Void> commitOffsetsAsync(final Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, final OffsetCommitCallback callback) {\n1047:         invokeCompletedOffsetCommitCallbacks();\n1048: \n1049:         RequestFuture<Void> future = null;\n1050:         if (offsets.isEmpty()) {\n1051:             // No need to check coordinator if offsets is empty since commit of empty offsets is completed locally.\n1052:             future = doCommitOffsetsAsync(offsets, callback);\n1053:         } else if (!coordinatorUnknownAndUnreadyAsync()) {\n1054:             // we need to make sure coordinator is ready before committing, since\n1055:             // this is for async committing we do not try to block, but just try once to\n1056:             // clear the previous discover-coordinator future, resend, or get responses;\n1057:             // if the coordinator is not ready yet then we would just proceed and put that into the\n1058:             // pending requests, and future poll calls would still try to complete them.\n1059:             //\n1060:             // the key here though is that we have to try sending the discover-coordinator if\n1061:             // it's not known or ready, since this is the only place we can send such request\n1062:             // under manual assignment (there we would not have heartbeat thread trying to auto-rediscover\n1063:             // the coordinator).\n1064:             future = doCommitOffsetsAsync(offsets, callback);\n1065:         } else {\n1066:             // we don't know the current coordinator, so try to find it and then send the commit\n1067:             // or fail (we don't want recursive retries which can cause offset commits to arrive\n1068:             // out of order). Note that there may be multiple offset commits chained to the same\n1069:             // coordinator lookup request. This is fine because the listeners will be invoked in\n1070:             // the same order that they were added. Note also that AbstractCoordinator prevents\n1071:             // multiple concurrent coordinator lookup requests.\n1072:             pendingAsyncCommits.incrementAndGet();\n1073:             lookupCoordinator().addListener(new RequestFutureListener<>() {\n1074:                 @Override\n1075:                 public void onSuccess(Void value) {\n1076:                     pendingAsyncCommits.decrementAndGet();\n1077:                     doCommitOffsetsAsync(offsets, callback);\n1078:                     client.pollNoWakeup();\n1079:                 }\n1080: \n1081:                 @Override\n1082:                 public void onFailure(RuntimeException e) {\n1083:                     pendingAsyncCommits.decrementAndGet();\n1084:                     completedOffsetCommits.add(new OffsetCommitCompletion(callback, offsets,\n1085:                             new RetriableCommitFailedException(e)));\n1086:                 }\n1087:             });\n1088:         }\n1089: \n1090:         // ensure the commit has a chance to be transmitted (without blocking on its completion).\n1091:         // Note that commits are treated as heartbeats by the coordinator, so there is no need to\n1092:         // explicitly allow heartbeats through delayed task execution.\n1093:         client.pollNoWakeup();\n1094:         return future;\n1095:     }\n1096: \n1097:     private RequestFuture<Void> doCommitOffsetsAsync(final Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, final OffsetCommitCallback callback) {\n1098:         RequestFuture<Void> future = sendOffsetCommitRequest(offsets);\n1099:         inFlightAsyncCommits.incrementAndGet();\n1100:         final OffsetCommitCallback cb = callback == null ? If so, ensure that\n1159:             // the corresponding callbacks are invoked prior to returning in order to preserve the order that\n1160:             // the offset commits were applied.\n1161:             invokeCompletedOffsetCommitCallbacks();\n1162: \n1163:             if (future.succeeded()) {\n1164:                 if (interceptors != null)\n1165:                     interceptors.onCommit(offsets);\n1166:                 return true;\n1167:             }\n1168: \n1169:             if (future.failed() && !future.isRetriable())\n1170:                 throw future.exception();\n1171: \n1172:             timer.sleep(retryBackoff.backoff(attempts++));\n1173:         } while (timer.notExpired());\n1174: \n1175:         return false;\n1176:     }\n1177: \n1178:     private void maybeAutoCommitOffsetsSync(Timer timer) {\n1179:         if (autoCommitEnabled) {\n1180:             Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> allConsumedOffsets = subscriptions.allConsumed();\n1181:             try {\n1182:                 log.debug(\"Sending synchronous auto-commit of offsets {}\", allConsumedOffsets);\n1183:                 if (!commitOffsetsSync(allConsumedOffsets, timer))\n1184:                     log.debug(\"Auto-commit of offsets {} timed out before completion\", allConsumedOffsets);\n1185:             } catch (WakeupException | InterruptException e) {\n1186:                 log.debug(\"Auto-commit of offsets {} was interrupted before completion\", allConsumedOffsets);\n1187:                 // rethrow wakeups since they are triggered by the user\n1188:                 throw e;\n1189:             } catch (Exception e) {\n1190:                 // consistent with async auto-commit failures, we do not }\n1195: \n1196:     public void maybeAutoCommitOffsetsAsync(long now) {\n1197:         if (autoCommitEnabled) {\n1198:             nextAutoCommitTimer.update(now);\n1199:             if }\n1204:     }\n1205: \n1206:     private boolean invokePendingAsyncCommits(Timer timer) {\n1207:         if (inFlightAsyncCommits.get() == 0) {\n1208:             return true;\n1209:         }\n1210:
